fence="true">]</mo></mrow><mrow><mn>2</mn><msup><mrow><mi>cosh</mi><mo>⁡</mo></mrow><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><msqrt><mfrac><msub><mi>r</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><mn>2</mn></mfrac></msqrt></mrow><mrow><mn>2</mn><msup><mrow><mi>cosh</mi><mo>⁡</mo></mrow><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><msqrt><mfrac><mi>r</mi><mn>2</mn></mfrac></msqrt></mrow></msubsup><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex"> \begin{align*} dL_0{}^2 &amp;= \left(\frac{r - 2}{r}\right)^{-1} dr^2, \\ dL_0 &amp;= \sqrt{\frac{r}{r - 2}} dr, \\ \int_0^{L_0} dL_0 &amp;= \int_{r_0}^r \sqrt{\frac{r}{r - 2}} dr, \\ L_0 &amp;= \int_{r_0}^r \sqrt{\frac{r}{r - 2}} dr, \\ r &amp;= u^2, \\ dr &amp;= 2u\ du, \\ u &amp;= \sqrt{r}, \\ L_0 &amp;= \int_{\sqrt{r_0}}^{\sqrt{r}} \sqrt{\frac{u^2}{u^2 - 2}} 2u\ du \\ &amp;= 2 \int_{\sqrt{r_0}}^{\sqrt{r}} \frac{u^2}{\sqrt{u^2 - 2}} du, \\ u &amp;= \sqrt{2} y, \\ du &amp;= \sqrt{2}\ dy, \\ y &amp;= \frac{u}{\sqrt{2}}, \\ L_0 &amp;= 2 \int_{\sqrt{\frac{r_0}{2}}}^{\sqrt{\frac{r}{2}}} \frac{2y^2}{\sqrt{2y^2 - 2}} \sqrt{2}\ dy \\ &amp;= 4 \int_{\sqrt{\frac{r_0}{2}}}^{\sqrt{\frac{r}{2}}} \frac{y^2}{\sqrt{2} \sqrt{y^2 - 1}} \sqrt{2}\ dy \\ &amp;= 4 \int_{\sqrt{\frac{r_0}{2}}}^{\sqrt{\frac{r}{2}}} \frac{y^2}{\sqrt{y^2 - 1}} dy, \\ y &amp;= \cosh \alpha, \\ dy &amp;= \sinh \alpha\ d\alpha, \\ \alpha &amp;= \cosh^{-1} y, \\ L_0 &amp;= 4 \int_{\cosh^{-1} \sqrt{\frac{r_0}{2}}}^{\cosh^{-1} \sqrt{\frac{r}{2}}} \frac{\cosh^2 {\alpha}}{\sqrt{\cosh^2 \alpha - 1}} \sinh \alpha\ d\alpha \\ &amp;= 4 \int_{\cosh^{-1} \sqrt{\frac{r_0}{2}}}^{\cosh^{-1} \sqrt{\frac{r}{2}}} \cosh^2 {\alpha}\ d\alpha \\ &amp;= 4 \int_{\cosh^{-1} \sqrt{\frac{r_0}{2}}}^{\cosh^{-1} \sqrt{\frac{r}{2}}} \frac{\cosh 2\alpha + 1}{2} d\alpha \\ &amp;= \int_{\cosh^{-1} \sqrt{\frac{r_0}{2}}}^{\cosh^{-1} \sqrt{\frac{r}{2}}} 2 (\cosh 2\alpha + 1)\ d\alpha, \\ \beta &amp;= 2 \alpha, \\ d\beta &amp;= 2\ d\alpha, \\ L_0 &amp;= \int_{2\cosh^{-1} \sqrt{\frac{r_0}{2}}}^{2\cosh^{-1} \sqrt{\frac{r}{2}}} (\cosh \beta + 1)\ d\beta \\ &amp;= \left[\sinh \beta + \beta\right]_{2\cosh^{-1} \sqrt{\frac{r_0}{2}}}^{2\cosh^{-1} \sqrt{\frac{r}{2}}}. \\ \end{align*} </annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span 2}{r}\right)^{-1} dr^2 &amp;= \left(\left(\frac{dz}{dr}\right)^2 + 1\right) dr^2, \\ \left(\frac{dz}{dr}\right)^2 + 1 &amp;= \frac{r}{r - 2}, \\ \left(\frac{dz}{dr}\right)^2 &amp;= \frac{r}{r - 2} - 1
